### Adjusted IQR ë°©ë²•ë¡  ê°œìš”

**ê³„ì‚° ê³µì‹:**
- Bowley ì™œë„: `(Q3 + Q1 - 2Ã—Median) / IQR`
- ì–‘ì˜ ì™œë„ (Right-skewed):

  - Upper Mult = exp(+c Ã— skew)
- ìŒì˜ ì™œë„ (Left-skewed):

- Adjusted Bounds: Q1 - 1.5Ã—IQRÃ—Lower_Mult, Q3 + 1.5Ã—IQRÃ—Upper_Mult
